PROMPT:
You are playing Settlers of Catan. Your task is to analyze the game state and choose the best action from the available options.

Rules:
1. Think through your decision step by step, analyzing the game state, resources, and available actions
2. Your aim is to WIN. That means 10 victory points.
3. Put your final chosen action inside a box like \boxed{5}
4. Your final answer must be a single integer corresponding to the action number
5. If you want to create or update your strategic plan, put it in <plan> tags like:
   <plan>Build roads toward port, then build settlement at node 13, then focus on city upgrades</plan>
6. Analyze the recent resource changes to understand what resources you're collecting effectively
7. Think about the next 2-3 turns, not just the immediate action

Strategies for Winning:

### Early Game Placement:
- Prioritize resource variety across your first two settlements. Ensure you have access to wood, brick, wheat, ore, and sheep, or at least a balanced subset.
- Place settlements on high-probability dice numbers (6, 8, or 9) for consistent resource income.
- Strategically position roads to secure future settlement spots that either maximize resource diversity or provide a path to critical ports.
- Avoid congested areas and focus on expanding toward less contested areas.
- Be mindful of opponent placements to cut off their expansion opportunities or secure key nodes first.

### Mid-Game Resource and Expansion:
- Monitor resource production tendencies and adjust your focus accordingly (e.g., prioritize wheat and ore for cities or wood and brick for roads).
- Utilize trades (both player trades and ports) to address shortages and accelerate expansion plans.
- Expand settlements to locations with valuable resources or strategic advantages, such as ports or high-probability hexes.

### Development Card Usage:
- Strategically buy development cards to secure the Largest Army or gain tactical advantages (e.g., using knights to move the robber or monopoly cards to dominate a specific resource).
- Save development cards for pivotal moments when they can shift the game in your favor.

### Late-Game Victory Point Optimization:
- Upgrade settlements to cities on high-yield tiles to maximize resource production.
- Leverage Longest Road and Largest Army for additional victory points when they can be feasibly secured.
- Consider alternative VP sources such as Victory Point cards.

Board Understanding Guide:
- The RESOURCE & NODE GRID shows hexagonal tiles with their coordinates, resources, and dice numbers
- The nodes connected to each tile are listed below each tile
- ğŸ” marks the robber's location, blocking resource production on that hex
- Settlements/cities and their production are listed in the BUILDINGS section
- Understanding the connectivity between nodes is crucial for road building strategy
- Ports allow trading resources at better rates (2:1 or 3:1)

### Step 1: Review Current Plan
Current plan: 
* Build settlement at node 3.
* Use initial roads to expand toward a port or strategic node (e.g., nodes near wheat and ore).
* Focus on securing cities and development cards in mid-game.

### Step 2: Evaluate the Game State
**Board Analysis:**
- ğŸ”µ Blue's settlement is at node 6, producing ğŸŒ²6 [â­â­â­] and â›ï¸3 [â­]. This is a strong start for wood but weak for wheat and brick.
- ğŸ”´ Red's settlement is at node 2, producing ğŸŒ²6 [â­â­â­], ğŸŒ¾4 [â­], and ğŸ§±10 [â­].
  - They have slightly better diversity due to access to wheat and brick. However, their low production numbers (1 vs. 3 dice probabilities in some cases) may leave them resource-constrained early on.

**Port Strategy:**
- Ports are critical, especially as we lack immediate wheat and brick. Building settlements toward ports will help reduce trading inefficiencies. None are close yet, but long-term port access is necessary.

**Primary Goal:**
- For our initial road placement, opt for roads that expand toward a potential useful settlement location. Node connections near wheat and ore are particularly attractive since cities rely heavily on these resources.

### Step 3: Examine Road Options
Here are the road-building choices:

1. **[0] Build road at edge (6, 23):**
   - This moves toward node 23, connecting to ore (â›ï¸3).
   - It gives access to a future settlement or expansion toward ports/other areas.
   - While not immediately game-changing, it complements our ore production and eventual strategy to build cities.

2. **[1] Build road at edge (1, 6):**
   - This points toward node 1, where ğŸŒ¾4 wheat and ğŸ‘5 sheep are present.
   - Wheat is crucial for cities and development cards. However, due to low production numbers on the tiles (4 and 5), this road's benefit may take time to realize.

3. **[2] Build road at edge (6, 7):**
   - This road goes toward node 7, adjacent to ğŸŒ²6 and ğŸ‘5. However, this does not expand toward unique resources and worsens resource redundancy (since we're already strong on wood ğŸŒ²6).

### Step 4: Evaluate Mid-Game and Long-Term Plans
- Node 23 is appealing because ore is critical for cities in the mid-game.
- Node 1 is also appealing, offering eventual access to wheat and sheep, both essential for settlements and development cards.
- Node 7 would duplicate wood production, which is unnecessary at this stage.

**Optimal Option:** Building the road toward node 23 strikes a balance between increasing valuable resource access and fulfilling the strategy outlined in the plan. It sets us up for future cities and development cards focus.

PROMPT:
You are playing Settlers of Catan. Your task is to analyze the game state and choose the best action from the available options.

Rules:
1. Think through your decision step by step, analyzing the game state, resources, and available actions
2. Your aim is to WIN. That means 10 victory points.
3. Put your final chosen action inside a box like \boxed{5}
4. Your final answer must be a single integer corresponding to the action number
5. If you want to create or update your strategic plan, put it in <plan> tags like:
   <plan>Build roads toward port, then build settlement at node 13, then focus on city upgrades</plan>
6. Analyze the recent resource changes to understand what resources you're collecting effectively
7. Think about the next 2-3 turns, not just the immediate action

Strategies for Winning:

### Early Game Placement:
- Prioritize resource variety across your first two settlements. Ensure you have access to wood, brick, wheat, ore, and sheep, or at least a balanced subset.
- Place settlements on high-probability dice numbers (6, 8, or 9) for consistent resource income.
- Strategically position roads to secure future settlement spots that either maximize resource diversity or provide a path to critical ports.
- Avoid congested areas and focus on expanding toward less contested areas.
- Be mindful of opponent placements to cut off their expansion opportunities or secure key nodes first.

### Mid-Game Resource and Expansion:
- Monitor resource production tendencies and adjust your focus accordingly (e.g., prioritize wheat and ore for cities or wood and brick for roads).
- Utilize trades (both player trades and ports) to address shortages and accelerate expansion plans.
- Expand settlements to locations with valuable resources or strategic advantages, such as ports or high-probability hexes.

### Development Card Usage:
- Strategically buy development cards to secure the Largest Army or gain tactical advantages (e.g., using knights to move the robber or monopoly cards to dominate a specific resource).
- Save development cards for pivotal moments when they can shift the game in your favor.

### Late-Game Victory Point Optimization:
- Upgrade settlements to cities on high-yield tiles to maximize resource production.
- Leverage Longest Road and Largest Army for additional victory points when they can be feasibly secured.
- Consider alternative VP sources such as Victory Point cards.

- Leverage Longest Road and Largest Army for additional victory points when they can be feasibly secured.

Strategies for Winning:

### Early Game Placement:
- Prioritize resource variety across your first two settlements. Ensure you have access to wood, brick, wheat, ore, and sheep, or at least a balanced subset.
- Place settlements on high-probability dice numbers (6, 8, or 9) for consistent resource income.
- Strategically position roads to secure future settlement spots that either maximize resource diversity or provide a path to critical ports.
- Avoid congested areas and focus on expanding toward less contested areas.
- Be mindful of opponent placements to cut off their expansion opportunities or secure key nodes first.

### Mid-Game Resource and Expansion:
- Monitor resource production tendencies and adjust your focus accordingly (e.g., prioritize wheat and ore for cities or wood and brick for roads).
- Utilize trades (both player trades and ports) to address shortages and accelerate expansion plans.
- Expand settlements to locations with valuable resources or strategic advantages, such as ports or high-probability hexes.

### Development Card Usage:
- Strategically buy development cards to secure the Largest Army or gain tactical advantages (e.g., using knights to move the robber or monopoly cards to dominate a specific resource).
- Save development cards for pivotal moments when they can shift the game in your favor.

### Late-Game Victory Point Optimization:
- Upgrade settlements to cities on high-yield tiles to maximize resource production.
- Leverage Longest Road and Largest Army for additional victory points when they can be feasibly secured.
- Consider alternative VP sources such as Victory Point cards.

- Avoid congested areas and focus on expanding toward less contested areas.
- Be mindful of opponent placements to cut off their expansion opportunities or secure key nodes first.

### Mid-Game Resource and Expansion:
- Monitor resource production tendencies and adjust your focus accordingly (e.g., prioritize wheat and ore for cities or wood and brick for roads).
- Utilize trades (both player trades and ports) to address shortages and accelerate expansion plans.
- Expand settlements to locations with valuable resources or strategic advantages, such as ports or high-probability hexes.

- Strategically buy development cards to secure the Largest Army or gain tactical advantages (e.g., using knights to move the robber or monopoly cards to dominate a specific resource).
- Save development cards for pivotal moments when they can shift the game in your favor.

### Late-Game Victory Point Optimization:
- Upgrade settlements to cities on high-yield tiles to maximize resource production.
- Leverage Longest Road and Largest Army for additional victory points when they can be feasibly secured.
- Consider alternative VP sources such as Victory Point cards.

Strategies for Winning:

### Early Game Placement:
- Prioritize resource variety across your first two settlements. Ensure you have access to wood, brick, wheat, ore, and sheep, or at least a balanced subset.
- Place settlements on high-probability dice numbers (6, 8, or 9) for consistent resource income.
- Strategically position roads to secure future settlement spots that either maximize resource diversity or provide a path to critical ports.
- Avoid congested areas and focus on expanding toward less contested areas.
- Be mindful of opponent placements to cut off their expansion opportunities or secure key nodes first.

### Mid-Game Resource and Expansion:
- Monitor resource production tendencies and adjust your focus accordingly (e.g., prioritize wheat and ore for cities or wood and brick for roads).
- Utilize trades (both player trades and ports) to address shortages and accelerate expansion plans.
- Expand settlements to locations with valuable resources or strategic advantages, such as ports or high-probability hexes.

### Development Card Usage:
- Strategically buy development cards to secure the Largest Army or gain tactical advantages (e.g., using knights to move the robber or monopoly cards to dominate a specific resource).
- Save development cards for pivotal moments when they can shift the game in your favor.

### Late-Game Victory Point Optimization:
- Upgrade settlements to cities on high-yield tiles to maximize resource production.
- Leverage Longest Road and Largest Army for additional victory points when they can be feasibly secured.
- Consider alternative VP sources such as Victory Point cards.
